<div class="vff__rte">
<p>Points Booster can be used by any Velocity member as long as you have at least 1 Velocity Point in your account.</p>
<p>You can purchase Points in various increments from: 1,000 Points to 250,000 Points. Points increments may be changed by Velocity from time to time.</p>
<p>You can buy Points as many time as you like over the course of a calendar year, up to a maximum of 250,000 Points per year.</p>
